python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo

docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id

sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload

top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests

requests.get('https://example.com')

git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests

import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()
ls -lh
find . -name "*.py"
grep -r "TODO" .
top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot

touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests
python3
import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()
ls -lh
find . -name "*.py"
grep -r "TODO" .
top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx

rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests
python3
import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()

top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh

cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub

sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'

sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx

sudo apt autoremove -y

cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh

sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh

cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc

sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m

kill -9 1234
history
clear

traceroute github.com

ifconfig
sudo reboot

cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests

import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()

top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit

cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog

sudo systemctl status nginx

cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests
python3
import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()
ls -lh
find . -name "*.py"
grep -r "TODO" .
top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y

deactivate

sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc

sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py

clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit

cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog

sudo systemctl status nginx

cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub

sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl

man ls

nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py

clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit

cat syslog

sudo systemctl status nginx

ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests
python3
import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()

grep -r "TODO" .
top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit

cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx

ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh

cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..

python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo

docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id

sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload

top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests

requests.get('https://example.com')

git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests

import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()
ls -lh
find . -name "*.py"
grep -r "TODO" .
top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot

touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests
python3
import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()
ls -lh
find . -name "*.py"
grep -r "TODO" .
top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx

rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests
python3
import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()

top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh

cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub

sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'

sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx

sudo apt autoremove -y

cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh

sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh

cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc

sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m

kill -9 1234
history
clear

traceroute github.com

ifconfig
sudo reboot

cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests

import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()

top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit

cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog

sudo systemctl status nginx

cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests
python3
import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()
ls -lh
find . -name "*.py"
grep -r "TODO" .
top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y

deactivate

sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc

sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py

clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit

cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog

sudo systemctl status nginx

cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub

sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl

man ls

nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py

clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit

cat syslog

sudo systemctl status nginx

ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests
python3
import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()

grep -r "TODO" .
top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit

cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx

ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh

cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..

python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo

docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id

sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload

top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests

requests.get('https://example.com')

git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests

import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()
ls -lh
find . -name "*.py"
grep -r "TODO" .
top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot

touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests
python3
import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()
ls -lh
find . -name "*.py"
grep -r "TODO" .
top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx

rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests
python3
import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()

top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh

cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub

sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'

sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx

sudo apt autoremove -y

git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests
python3
import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()
ls -lh
find . -name "*.py"
grep -r "TODO" .
top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh

pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh

nano script.sh

lsmem

lsmem

ls -lh
find . -name "*.py"
grep -r "TODO" .
top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh

cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature

git commit -m "Initial commit"

cd ..

sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls

sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit

cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx

rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests
python3
import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()

top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh

cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub

sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'

sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx

sudo apt autoremove -y

cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh

sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh

cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc

sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m

kill -9 1234
history
clear

traceroute github.com

ifconfig
sudo reboot

cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests

import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()

top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit

cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog

sudo systemctl status nginx

cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests
python3
import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()
ls -lh
find . -name "*.py"
grep -r "TODO" .
top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y

deactivate

sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc

sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py

clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit

cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog

sudo systemctl status nginx

cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub

sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl

man ls

nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py

clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit

cat syslog

sudo systemctl status nginx

ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests
python3
import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()

grep -r "TODO" .
top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
history -c
cd ~/projects
ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit

cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx

ls -la
git status
vim main.py
python3 main.py
clear
htop
sudo apt update
sudo apt upgrade -y
exit
ssh user@192.168.1.10
cd /var/log
cat syslog
tail -f /var/log/syslog
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl status nginx
cd ~
mkdir test_folder
cd test_folder
touch file1.txt
echo "Hello World" > file1.txt
cat file1.txt
rm file1.txt
cd ..
rmdir test_folder
pwd
lsblk
df -h
free -m
ps aux | grep python
kill -9 1234
history
clear
cd ~/Downloads
wget https://example.com/file.zip
unzip file.zip
rm file.zip
cd ~
sudo nano /etc/hosts
ping google.com
traceroute github.com
curl https://api.ipify.org
ifconfig
sudo reboot
cd ~/scripts
chmod +x backup.sh
./backup.sh
git clone https://github.com/example/repo.git
cd repo
git checkout -b new-feature
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"
git push origin new-feature
cd ..
rm -rf repo
docker ps
docker images
docker run -it ubuntu bash
docker stop container_id
docker rm container_id
sudo ufw status
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22
sudo ufw reload
sudo apt install python3-pip -y
pip3 install requests
python3
import requests
requests.get('https://example.com')
exit()
ls -lh
find . -name "*.py"
grep -r "TODO" .
top
sudo dmesg | less
history | grep ssh
ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 4096
cat ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub
sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser
sudo su - newuser
whoami
hostnamectl
uptime
man ls
alias ll='ls -la'
source ~/.bashrc
cd /etc
ls
sudo cp /etc/nginx/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf.bak
sudo systemctl reload nginx
nc -zv 127.0.0.1 80
sudo apt remove apache2 -y
sudo apt autoremove -y
python3 -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate
deactivate
rm -rf venv
echo $PATH
export PATH=$PATH:~/bin
mkdir -p ~/bin
cd ~/bin
touch script.sh
chmod +x script.sh
nano script.sh
bash script.sh
cd ~
ssh-copy-id user@192.168.1.10
rsync -avz ~/projects/ user@192.168.1.10:/home/user/projects/
lsusb
lscpu
lsmem
sudo lsof -i :80
curl -I https://www.example.com
